     371             : 
     372             : /* This routine should almost never be called now. It uses a flawed algorithm */
     373             : /*  which won't produce the best results. It gets called only when the better */
     374             : /*  approach doesn't work (singular matrices, etc.) */
     375             : /* Old comment, back when I was confused... */
     376             : /* Least squares tells us that:
     377             :         | S(xi*ti^3) |   | S(ti^6) S(ti^5) S(ti^4) S(ti^3) |   | a |
     378             :         | S(xi*ti^2) | = | S(ti^5) S(ti^4) S(ti^3) S(ti^2) | * | b |
     379             :         | S(xi*ti)   |   | S(ti^4) S(ti^3) S(ti^2) S(ti)   |   | c |
     380             :         | S(xi)      |   | S(ti^3) S(ti^2) S(ti)   n       |   | d |
     381             :  and the definition of a spline tells us:
     382             :         | x1         | = |   1        1       1       1    | * (a b c d)
     383             :         | x0         | = |   0        0       0       1    | * (a b c d)
     384             : So we're a bit over specified. Let's use the last two lines of least squares
     385             : and the 2 from the spline defn. So d==x0. Now we've got three unknowns
     386             : and only three equations...
     387             : 
     388             : For order2 splines we've got
     389             :         | S(xi*ti^2) |   | S(ti^4) S(ti^3) S(ti^2) |   | b |
     390             :         | S(xi*ti)   | = | S(ti^3) S(ti^2) S(ti)   | * | c |
     391             :         | S(xi)      |   | S(ti^2) S(ti)   n       |   | d |
     392             :  and the definition of a spline tells us:
     393             :         | x1         | = |   1       1       1    | * (b c d)
     394             :         | x0         | = |   0       0       1    | * (b c d)
     395             : =>
     396             :     d = x0
     397             :     b+c = x1-x0
     398             :     S(ti^2)*b + S(ti)*c = S(xi)-n*x0
     399             :     S(ti^2)*b + S(ti)*(x1-x0-b) = S(xi)-n*x0
     400             :     [ S(ti^2)-S(ti) ]*b = S(xi)-S(ti)*(x1-x0) - n*x0
     401             : */
     402           3 : static int _ApproximateSplineFromPoints(SplinePoint *from, SplinePoint *to,

     595             : /* Find a spline which best approximates the list of intermediate points we */

     600             : /* OK, we know the end points, so all we really need are the control points */
     601             :   /*    For cubics.... */
     602             : /* Pf = point from */
     603             : /* CPf = control point, from nextcp */
     604             : /* CPt = control point, to prevcp */
     605             : /* Pt = point to */
     606             : /* S(t) = Pf + 3*(CPf-Pf)*t + 3*(CPt-2*CPf+Pf)*t^2 + (Pt-3*CPt+3*CPf-Pf)*t^3 */
     607             : /* S(t) = Pf - 3*Pf*t + 3*Pf*t^2 - Pf*t^3 + Pt*t^3 +                         */
     608             : /*           3*(t-2*t^2+t^3)*CPf +                                           */
     609             : /*           3*(t^2-t^3)*CPt                                                 */
     610             : /* We want to minimize Σ [S(ti)-Pi]^2 */
     611             : /* There are four variables CPf.x, CPf.y, CPt.x, CPt.y */
     612             : /* When we take the derivative of the error term above with each of these */
     613             : /*  variables, we find that the two coordinates are separate. So I shall only */
     614             : /*  work through the equations once, leaving off the coordinate */
     615             : /* d error/dCPf = Σ 2*3*(t-2*t^2+t^3) * [S(ti)-Pi] = 0 */
     616             : /* d error/dCPt = Σ 2*3*(t^2-t^3)     * [S(ti)-Pi] = 0 */

     618             : /* CP = control point, there's only one */
     619             : /* S(t) = Pf + 2*(CP-Pf)*t + (Pt-2*CP+Pf)*t^2 */
     620             : /* S(t) = Pf - 2*Pf*t + Pf*t^2 + Pt*t^2 +     */
     621             : /*           2*(t-2*t^2)*CP                   */
     622             : /* We want to minimize Σ [S(ti)-Pi]^2 */
     623             : /* There are two variables CP.x, CP.y */
     624             : /* d error/dCP = Σ 2*2*(t-2*t^2) * [S(ti)-Pi] = 0 */
     625             : /* Σ (t-2*t^2) * [Pf - 2*Pf*t + Pf*t^2 + Pt*t^2 - Pi +     */
     626             : /*           2*(t-2*t^2)*CP] = 0               */
     627             : /* CP * (Σ 2*(t-2*t^2)*(t-2*t^2)) = Σ (t-2*t^2) * [Pf - 2*Pf*t + Pf*t^2 + Pt*t^2 - Pi] */

     629             : /*        Σ (t-2*t^2) * [Pf - 2*Pf*t + Pf*t^2 + Pt*t^2 - Pi] */

     875             : /* pf == point from (start point) */
     876             : /* Δf == slope from (cp(from) - from) */
     877             : /* pt == point to (end point, t==1) */
     878             : /* Δt == slope to (cp(to) - to) */
     879             : 
     880             : /* A spline from pf to pt with slope vectors rf*Δf, rt*Δt is: */
     881             : /* p(t) = pf +  [ 3*rf*Δf ]*t  +  3*[pt-pf+rt*Δt-2*rf*Δf] *t^2 +                     */
     882             : /*              [2*pf-2*pt+3*rf*Δf-3*rt*Δt]*t^3 */
     883             : 
     884             : /* So I want */
     885             : /*   d  Σ (p(t(i))-p(i))^2/ d rf  == 0 */
     886             : /*   d  Σ (p(t(i))-p(i))^2/ d rt  == 0 */
     887             : /* now... */
     888             : /*   d  Σ (p(t(i))-p(i))^2/ d rf  == 0 */
     889             : /* => Σ 3*t*Δf*(1-2*t+t^2)*
     890             :  *                      [pf-pi+ 3*(pt-pf)*t^2 + 2*(pf-pt)*t^3]   +
     891             :  *                      3*[t - 2*t^2 + t^3]*Δf*rf   +
     892             :  *                      3*[t^2-t^3]*Δt*rt   */
     893             : /* and... */
     894             : /*   d  Σ (p(t(i))-p(i))^2/ d rt  == 0 */
     895             : /* => Σ 3*t^2*Δt*(1-t)*
     896             :  *                      [pf-pi+ 3*(pt-pf)*t^2 + 2*(pf-pt)*t^3]   +
     897             :  *                      3*[t - 2*t^2 + t^3]*Δf*rf   +
     898             :  *                      3*[t^2-t^3]*Δt*rt   */
     899             : 
     900             : /* Now for a long time I looked at that and saw four equations and two unknowns*/
     901             : /*  That was I was trying to solve for x and y separately, and that doesn't work. */
     902             : /*  There are really just two equations and each sums over both x and y components */
     903             : 
     904             : /* Old comment: */
     905             : /* I used to do a least squares aproach adding two more to the above set of equations */
     906             : /*  which held the slopes constant. But that didn't work very well. So instead*/
